## Colleges 
- IPEDS
    - Directory
        - **unitid**, integer
            - Unit ID number
            - Special values
                - -1—Missing/not reported
                - -2—Not applicable
                - -3—Suppressed data
        - **year**, integer

                - -2—Not applicable

        - **inst_status**, integer
            - Status of institution
            - Special values
                - 1—Active
                - 2—[Unknown]
                - 3—Combined with other institution

                - 5—Perfect child campus
                - 6—Inactive due to hurricane related problems

                - 9—Out of scope of the IPEDS universe
                - 10—Potential new/add institution
                - 11—Potential restore institution
                - 12—Restore (active), restored to the current universe
                - 13—Split into more than one institution
                - 14—Duplicate, unit ID previously assigned
                - 15—Wipe out, out of scope, potential add
                - 16—Potential restore not within scope of IPEDS
                - 17—Universe III, out of scope

                    - -1—Missing/not reported
                    - -2—Not applicable
                    - -3—Suppressed data 
            - **campus_award_fed_contr_opeid**, float 
                - Federal contribution to campus awards by OPEID (dollars)
                - Special values
                    - -1—Missing/not reported
                    - -2—Not applicable
                    - -3—Suppressed data 
            - **allocation_flag**, integer
                - Recipients and disbursements are allocated across multiple unit IDs per OPEID
                - Special values
                    - 0—No
                    - 1—Yes
                    - -1—Missing/not reported
                    - -2—Not applicable
                    - -3—Suppressed data
            - **combined_flag**, integer
                - Indicates whether data from multiple OPEIDs have been combined into one unit ID
                - Special values
                    - 0—No
                    - 1—Yes
                    - -1—Missing/not reported
                    - -2—Not applicable
                    - -3—Suppressed data
            - **other_assoc_opeids**, string
                - Other OPEIDs associated with the same unit ID whose data have been combined
                - Special values
                    - -1—Missing/not reported
                    - -2—Not applicable
                    - -3—Suppressed data
